[ci/cargo-deny-advisories       ]   |    [0m[36m┌─[0m /mnt/4tbc/home/mnabil/LLM4Build/project_path/gitoxide/Cargo.lock:29:1
[ci/cargo-deny-advisories       ]   |    [0m[36m│[0m
[ci/cargo-deny-advisories       ]   | [0m[36m29[0m [0m[36m│[0m [0m[31maws-lc-sys 0.37.1 registry+https://github.com/rust-lang/crates.io-index[0m
[ci/cargo-deny-advisories       ]   |    [0m[36m│[0m [0m[31m━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━[0m [0m[31msecurity vulnerability detected[0m
[ci/cargo-deny-advisories       ]   |    [0m[36m│[0m
[ci/cargo-deny-advisories       ]   |    [0m[36m├[0m ID: RUSTSEC-2026-0044
[ci/cargo-deny-advisories       ]   |    [0m[36m├[0m Advisory: https://rustsec.org/advisories/RUSTSEC-2026-0044
[ci/cargo-deny-advisories       ]   |    [0m[36m├[0m A logic error in CN (Common Name) validation allows certificates with
[ci/cargo-deny-advisories       ]   |      wildcard or raw UTF-8 Unicode CN values to bypass name constraints
[ci/cargo-deny-advisories       ]   |      enforcement. The `cn2dnsid` function does not recognize these CN patterns
[ci/cargo-deny-advisories       ]   |      as valid DNS identifiers, causing `NAME_CONSTRAINTS_check_CN` to skip
[ci/cargo-deny-advisories       ]   |      validation. However, `X509_check_host` accepts these CN values when no
[ci/cargo-deny-advisories       ]   |      dNSName SAN is present, allowing certificates to bypass name constraints
[ci/cargo-deny-advisories       ]   |      while still being used for hostname verification.
[ci/cargo-deny-advisories       ]   |      
[ci/cargo-deny-advisories       ]   |      Customers of AWS services do not need to take action. Applications using
[ci/cargo-deny-advisories       ]   |      `aws-lc-sys` should upgrade to the most recent release of `aws-lc-sys`.
[ci/cargo-deny-advisories       ]   |      
[ci/cargo-deny-advisories       ]   |      ## Workarounds
[ci/cargo-deny-advisories       ]   |      
[ci/cargo-deny-advisories       ]   |      Applications that set `X509_CHECK_FLAG_NEVER_CHECK_SUBJECT` to disable CN
[ci/cargo-deny-advisories       ]   |      fallback are not affected. Applications that only encounter certificates
[ci/cargo-deny-advisories       ]   |      with dNSName SANs (standard for public WebPKI) are also not affected.
[ci/cargo-deny-advisories       ]   |      
[ci/cargo-deny-advisories       ]   |      Otherwise, there is no workaround and applications using `aws-lc-sys` should
[ci/cargo-deny-advisories       ]   |      upgrade to the most recent releases of `aws-lc-sys`.
[ci/cargo-deny-advisories       ]   |    [0m[36m├[0m Solution: Upgrade to >=0.39.0 (try `cargo update -p aws-lc-sys`)

[ci/cargo-deny-advisories       ]   |    [0m[36m┌─[0m /mnt/4tbc/home/mnabil/LLM4Build/project_path/gitoxide/Cargo.lock:29:1
[ci/cargo-deny-advisories       ]   |    [0m[36m│[0m
[ci/cargo-deny-advisories       ]   | [0m[36m29[0m [0m[36m│[0m [0m[31maws-lc-sys 0.37.1 registry+https://github.com/rust-lang/crates.io-index[0m
[ci/cargo-deny-advisories       ]   |    [0m[36m│[0m [0m[31m━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━[0m [0m[31msecurity vulnerability detected[0m
[ci/cargo-deny-advisories       ]   |    [0m[36m│[0m
[ci/cargo-deny-advisories       ]   |    [0m[36m├[0m ID: RUSTSEC-2026-0045
[ci/cargo-deny-advisories       ]   |    [0m[36m├[0m Advisory: https://rustsec.org/advisories/RUSTSEC-2026-0045
[ci/cargo-deny-advisories       ]   |    [0m[36m├[0m Observable timing discrepancy in AES-CCM decryption in AWS-LC allows an
[ci/cargo-deny-advisories       ]   |      unauthenticated user to potentially determine authentication tag validity
[ci/cargo-deny-advisories       ]   |      via timing analysis.
[ci/cargo-deny-advisories       ]   |      
[ci/cargo-deny-advisories       ]   |      The impacted implementations are through the EVP CIPHER API:
[ci/cargo-deny-advisories       ]   |      `EVP_aes_128_ccm`, `EVP_aes_192_ccm`, and `EVP_aes_256_ccm`.
[ci/cargo-deny-advisories       ]   |      
[ci/cargo-deny-advisories       ]   |      Customers of AWS services do not need to take action. `aws-lc-sys` contains
[ci/cargo-deny-advisories       ]   |      code from AWS-LC. Applications using `aws-lc-sys` should upgrade to the most
[ci/cargo-deny-advisories       ]   |      recent release of `aws-lc-sys`.
[ci/cargo-deny-advisories       ]   |      
[ci/cargo-deny-advisories       ]   |      ## Workarounds
[ci/cargo-deny-advisories       ]   |      
[ci/cargo-deny-advisories       ]   |      In the special cases of using AES-CCM with (M=4, L=2), (M=8, L=2), or
[ci/cargo-deny-advisories       ]   |      (M=16, L=2), applications can workaround this issue by using AES-CCM through
[ci/cargo-deny-advisories       ]   |      the EVP AEAD API using implementations `EVP_aead_aes_128_ccm_bluetooth`,
[ci/cargo-deny-advisories       ]   |      `EVP_aead_aes_128_ccm_bluetooth_8`, and `EVP_aead_aes_128_ccm_matter`
[ci/cargo-deny-advisories       ]   |      respectively.
[ci/cargo-deny-advisories       ]   |      
[ci/cargo-deny-advisories       ]   |      Otherwise, there is no workaround and applications using `aws-lc-sys` should
[ci/cargo-deny-advisories       ]   |      upgrade to the most recent release.
[ci/cargo-deny-advisories       ]   |    [0m[36m├[0m Announcement: https://aws.amazon.com/security/security-bulletins/2026-005-AWS
[ci/cargo-deny-advisories       ]   |    [0m[36m├[0m Solution: Upgrade to >=0.38.0 (try `cargo update -p aws-lc-sys`)

[ci/cargo-deny-advisories       ]   | [0m[36m29[0m [0m[36m│[0m [0m[31maws-lc-sys 0.37.1 registry+https://github.com/rust-lang/crates.io-index[0m
[ci/cargo-deny-advisories       ]   |    [0m[36m│[0m [0m[31m━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━[0m [0m[31msecurity vulnerability detected[0m
[ci/cargo-deny-advisories       ]   |    [0m[36m│[0m
[ci/cargo-deny-advisories       ]   |    [0m[36m├[0m ID: RUSTSEC-2026-0048
[ci/cargo-deny-advisories       ]   |    [0m[36m├[0m Advisory: https://rustsec.org/advisories/RUSTSEC-2026-0048
[ci/cargo-deny-advisories       ]   |    [0m[36m├[0m A logic error in CRL distribution point matching in AWS-LC allows a revoked
[ci/cargo-deny-advisories       ]   |      certificate to bypass revocation checks during certificate validation, when
[ci/cargo-deny-advisories       ]   |      the application enables CRL checking and uses partitioned CRLs with Issuing
[ci/cargo-deny-advisories       ]   |      Distribution Point (IDP) extensions.
[ci/cargo-deny-advisories       ]   |      
[ci/cargo-deny-advisories       ]   |      Customers of AWS services do not need to take action. `aws-lc-sys` contains
[ci/cargo-deny-advisories       ]   |      code from AWS-LC. Applications using `aws-lc-sys` should upgrade to the most
[ci/cargo-deny-advisories       ]   |      recent release of `aws-lc-sys`.
[ci/cargo-deny-advisories       ]   |      
[ci/cargo-deny-advisories       ]   |      ## Workarounds
[ci/cargo-deny-advisories       ]   |      
[ci/cargo-deny-advisories       ]   |      Applications can workaround this issue if they do not enable CRL checking
[ci/cargo-deny-advisories       ]   |      (`X509_V_FLAG_CRL_CHECK`). Applications using complete (non-partitioned)
[ci/cargo-deny-advisories       ]   |      CRLs without IDP extensions are also not affected.
[ci/cargo-deny-advisories       ]   |      
[ci/cargo-deny-advisories       ]   |      Otherwise, there is no workaround and applications using `aws-lc-sys` should
[ci/cargo-deny-advisories       ]   |      upgrade to the most recent releases of `aws-lc-sys`.
[ci/cargo-deny-advisories       ]   |    [0m[36m├[0m Announcement: https://aws.amazon.com/security/security-bulletins/2026-010-AWS

[ci/cargo-deny-advisories       ]   | [0m[1m[38;5;9merror[vulnerability][0m[1m: CRLs not considered authoritative by Distribution Point due to faulty matching logic[0m
[ci/cargo-deny-advisories       ]   |     [0m[36m┌─[0m /mnt/4tbc/home/mnabil/LLM4Build/project_path/gitoxide/Cargo.lock:374:1
[ci/cargo-deny-advisories       ]   |     [0m[36m│[0m
[ci/cargo-deny-advisories       ]   | [0m[36m374[0m [0m[36m│[0m [0m[31mrustls-webpki 0.103.9 registry+https://github.com/rust-lang/crates.io-index[0m
[ci/cargo-deny-advisories       ]   |     [0m[36m│[0m [0m[31m━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━[0m [0m[31msecurity vulnerability detected[0m
[ci/cargo-deny-advisories       ]   |     [0m[36m│[0m
[ci/cargo-deny-advisories       ]   |     [0m[36m├[0m ID: RUSTSEC-2026-0049
[ci/cargo-deny-advisories       ]   |     [0m[36m├[0m Advisory: https://rustsec.org/advisories/RUSTSEC-2026-0049
[ci/cargo-deny-advisories       ]   |     [0m[36m├[0m If a certificate had more than one `distributionPoint`, then only the first `distributionPoint` would be considered against each CRL's `IssuingDistributionPoint` `distributionPoint`, and then the certificate's subsequent `distributionPoint`s would be ignored.
[ci/cargo-deny-advisories       ]   |       
[ci/cargo-deny-advisories       ]   |       The impact was that correctly provided CRLs would not be consulted to check revocation. With `UnknownStatusPolicy::Deny` (the default) this would lead to incorrect but safe `Error::UnknownRevocationStatus`. With `UnknownStatusPolicy::Allow` this would lead to inappropriate acceptance of revoked certificates.
[ci/cargo-deny-advisories       ]   |       
[ci/cargo-deny-advisories       ]   |       This vulnerability is thought to be of limited impact. This is because both the certificate and CRL are signed -- an attacker would need to compromise a trusted issuing authority to trigger this bug.  An attacker with such capabilities could likely bypass revocation checking through other more impactful means (such as publishing a valid, empty CRL.)
[ci/cargo-deny-advisories       ]   |       
[ci/cargo-deny-advisories       ]   |       More likely, this bug would be latent in normal use, and an attacker could leverage faulty revocation checking to continue using a revoked credential.
[ci/cargo-deny-advisories       ]   |       
[ci/cargo-deny-advisories       ]   |       This vulnerability is identified as [GHSA-pwjx-qhcg-rvj4](https://github.com/rustls/webpki/security/advisories/GHSA-pwjx-qhcg-rvj4). Thank you to @1seal for the report.

[ci/cargo-deny-advisories       ]   |     [0m[36m│[0m [0m[31m━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━[0m [0m[31msecurity vulnerability detected[0m

[ci/cargo-deny-advisories       ]   |

[ci/cargo-deny-advisories       ]   |

[ci/cargo-deny-advisories       ]   |     [0m[36m│[0m [0m[31m━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━[0m [0m[31msecurity vulnerability detected[0m
[ci/cargo-deny-advisories       ]   |     [0m[36m│[0m
[ci/cargo-deny-advisories       ]   |     [0m[36m├[0m ID: RUSTSEC-2026-0099
[ci/cargo-deny-advisories       ]   |     [0m[36m├[0m Advisory: https://rustsec.org/advisories/RUSTSEC-2026-0099
[ci/cargo-deny-advisories       ]   |     [0m[36m├[0m Permitted subtree name constraints for DNS names were accepted for certificates asserting a wildcard name.
[ci/cargo-deny-advisories       ]   |       
[ci/cargo-deny-advisories       ]   |       This was incorrect because, given a name constraint of `accept.example.com`, `*.example.com` could feasibly allow a name of `reject.example.com` which is outside the constraint.
[ci/cargo-deny-advisories       ]   |       This is very similar to [CVE-2025-61727](https://go.dev/issue/76442).
[ci/cargo-deny-advisories       ]   |       
[ci/cargo-deny-advisories       ]   |       Since name constraints are restrictions on otherwise properly-issued certificates, this bug is reachable only after signature verification and requires misissuance to exploit.
[ci/cargo-deny-advisories       ]   |       
[ci/cargo-deny-advisories       ]   |       This vulnerability is identified as [GHSA-xgp8-3hg3-c2mh](https://github.com/rustls/webpki/security/advisories/GHSA-xgp8-3hg3-c2mh). Thank you to @1seal for the report.

[ci/cargo-deny-advisories       ]   | [0m[1m[38;5;9merror[vulnerability][0m[1m: `unpack_in` can chmod arbitrary directories by following symlinks[0m
[ci/cargo-deny-advisories       ]   |     [0m[36m┌─[0m /mnt/4tbc/home/mnabil/LLM4Build/project_path/gitoxide/Cargo.lock:423:1
[ci/cargo-deny-advisories       ]   |     [0m[36m│[0m
[ci/cargo-deny-advisories       ]   | [0m[36m423[0m [0m[36m│[0m [0m[31mtar 0.4.44 registry+https://github.com/rust-lang/crates.io-index[0m
[ci/cargo-deny-advisories       ]   |     [0m[36m│[0m [0m[31m━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━[0m [0m[31msecurity vulnerability detected[0m
[ci/cargo-deny-advisories       ]   |     [0m[36m│[0m
[ci/cargo-deny-advisories       ]   |     [0m[36m├[0m ID: RUSTSEC-2026-0067
[ci/cargo-deny-advisories       ]   |     [0m[36m├[0m Advisory: https://rustsec.org/advisories/RUSTSEC-2026-0067
[ci/cargo-deny-advisories       ]   |     [0m[36m├[0m In versions 0.4.44 and below of tar-rs, when unpacking a tar archive, the tar
[ci/cargo-deny-advisories       ]   |       crate's `unpack_dir` function uses [`fs::metadata()`][fs-metadata] to check
[ci/cargo-deny-advisories       ]   |       whether a path that already exists is a directory. Because `fs::metadata()`
[ci/cargo-deny-advisories       ]   |       follows symbolic links, a crafted tarball containing a symlink entry followed
[ci/cargo-deny-advisories       ]   |       by a directory entry with the same name causes the crate to treat the symlink
[ci/cargo-deny-advisories       ]   |       target as a valid existing directory — and subsequently apply chmod to it. This
[ci/cargo-deny-advisories       ]   |       allows an attacker to modify the permissions of arbitrary directories outside
[ci/cargo-deny-advisories       ]   |       the extraction root.
[ci/cargo-deny-advisories       ]   |       
[ci/cargo-deny-advisories       ]   |       This issue has been fixed in version 0.4.45.
[ci/cargo-deny-advisories       ]   |       
[ci/cargo-deny-advisories       ]   |       [fs-metadata]: https://doc.rust-lang.org/std/fs/fn.metadata.html
[ci/cargo-deny-advisories       ]   |     [0m[36m├[0m Solution: Upgrade to >=0.4.45 (try `cargo update -p tar`)
[ci/cargo-deny-advisories       ]   |     [0m[36m├[0m tar v0.4.44

[ci/cargo-deny-advisories       ]   | [0m[1m[38;5;9merror[vulnerability][0m[1m: tar-rs incorrectly ignores PAX size headers if header size is nonzero[0m
[ci/cargo-deny-advisories       ]   |     [0m[36m┌─[0m /mnt/4tbc/home/mnabil/LLM4Build/project_path/gitoxide/Cargo.lock:423:1
[ci/cargo-deny-advisories       ]   |     [0m[36m│[0m
[ci/cargo-deny-advisories       ]   | [0m[36m423[0m [0m[36m│[0m [0m[31mtar 0.4.44 registry+https://github.com/rust-lang/crates.io-index[0m
[ci/cargo-deny-advisories       ]   |     [0m[36m│[0m [0m[31m━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━[0m [0m[31msecurity vulnerability detected[0m
[ci/cargo-deny-advisories       ]   |     [0m[36m│[0m
[ci/cargo-deny-advisories       ]   |     [0m[36m├[0m ID: RUSTSEC-2026-0068
[ci/cargo-deny-advisories       ]   |     [0m[36m├[0m Advisory: https://rustsec.org/advisories/RUSTSEC-2026-0068
[ci/cargo-deny-advisories       ]   |     [0m[36m├[0m Versions 0.4.44 and below of tar-rs have conditional logic that skips the PAX
[ci/cargo-deny-advisories       ]   |       size header in cases where the base header size is nonzero.
[ci/cargo-deny-advisories       ]   |       
[ci/cargo-deny-advisories       ]   |       As part of [CVE-2025-62518][astral-cve], the [astral-tokio-tar]
[ci/cargo-deny-advisories       ]   |       project was changed to correctly honor PAX size headers in the case where it
[ci/cargo-deny-advisories       ]   |       was different from the base header. This is almost the inverse of the
[ci/cargo-deny-advisories       ]   |       astral-tokio-tar issue.
[ci/cargo-deny-advisories       ]   |       
[ci/cargo-deny-advisories       ]   |       Any discrepancy in how tar parsers honor file size can be used to create
[ci/cargo-deny-advisories       ]   |       archives that appear differently when unpacked by different archivers. In this
[ci/cargo-deny-advisories       ]   |       case, the tar-rs (Rust tar) crate is an outlier in checking for the header size
[ci/cargo-deny-advisories       ]   |       — other tar parsers (including e.g. Go [`archive/tar`][go-tar]) unconditionally
[ci/cargo-deny-advisories       ]   |       use the PAX size override. This can affect anything that uses the tar crate to
[ci/cargo-deny-advisories       ]   |       parse archives and expects to have a consistent view with other parsers.
[ci/cargo-deny-advisories       ]   |       
[ci/cargo-deny-advisories       ]   |       This issue has been fixed in version 0.4.45.
[ci/cargo-deny-advisories       ]   |       
[ci/cargo-deny-advisories       ]   |       [astral-cve]: https://www.cve.org/CVERecord?id=CVE-2025-62518
[ci/cargo-deny-advisories       ]   |       [astral-tokio-tar]: https://github.com/astral-sh/tokio-tar
[ci/cargo-deny-advisories       ]   |       [go-tar]: https://pkg.go.dev/archive/tar
[ci/cargo-deny-advisories       ]   |     [0m[36m├[0m Solution: Upgrade to >=0.4.45 (try `cargo update -p tar`)
[ci/cargo-deny-advisories       ]   |     [0m[36m├[0m tar v0.4.44
